I've uploaded a code repository in the directory /testbed. Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
[Bug]: MERGE on partitioned table produces duplicate rows when partition value contains a space
### What happened?

When a partitioned Delta table is merged into repeatedly using an identical source, the operation should be idempotent. This works correctly when the partition column value contains no spaces. When it contains a space, every merge call appends new rows instead of updating existing ones, doubling the row count each time. **This behaviour was introduced in 1.5.0 and does not occur on 1.4.2.**

### **Observed behaviour**

num_target_files_removed is always 0 even when num_target_rows_updated is non-zero. The merge correctly identifies matched rows and writes a new file, but never removes the original file from the Delta log. Both files remain active, causing duplicates on every subsequent call.

### Expected behavior

The second identical merge should produce num_target_files_removed = 1 and leave the row count unchanged.

### Operating System

Windows

### Binding

Python

### Bindings Version

1.5.0, 1.4.2

### Steps to reproduce

```python
import os
import tempfile
import pyarrow as pa
from deltalake import DeltaTable

_TS = 1_704_067_200_000_000  # 2024-01-01 00:00:00 UTC in microseconds

def make_data(group):
    n = 3
    return pa.table({
        "group": pa.array([group] * n, type=pa.string()),
        "region": pa.array(["A", "B", "C"], type=pa.string()),
        "ts": pa.array([_TS] * n, type=pa.timestamp("us")),
        "val": pa.array([1.0, 2.0, 3.0], type=pa.float64()),
    })

def run(group, path):
    data = make_data(group)
    predicate = f"target.group = '{group}' AND target.region = source.region AND target.ts = source.ts"
    DeltaTable.create(table_uri=path, schema=data.schema, partition_by=["group"])
    dt = DeltaTable(path)
    for i in range(1, 3):
        dt.merge(source=data, predicate=predicate, source_alias="source", target_alias="target") \
          .when_matched_update_all().when_not_matched_insert_all().execute()
        dt.update_incremental()
        metrics = dt.history(1)[0]["operationMetrics"]
        print(f"  merge {i}: rows={dt.to_pandas().shape[0]}, files_removed={metrics.get('num_target_files_removed')}")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    with tempfile.TemporaryDirectory() as tmp:
        print("With space:")
        run("foo bar", os.path.join(tmp, "a"))
        print("Without space:")
        run("foo_bar", os.path.join(tmp, "b"))

```

### Relevant logs

```shell
With space:
  merge 1: rows=3, files_removed=0
  merge 2: rows=6, files_removed=0   <-- duplicate rows, should be 3
Without space:
  merge 1: rows=3, files_removed=0
  merge 2: rows=3, files_removed=1   <-- correct
```

</pr_description>

  1556	        }
  1557	    }
  1558	
  1559	    let source_count_metrics = source_count.metrics().unwrap();
  1560	    let target_count_metrics = op_count.metrics().unwrap();
  1561	    let scan_count_metrics = scan_count.metrics().unwrap();
  1562	
  1563	    metrics.num_source_rows = get_metric(&source_count_metrics, SOURCE_COUNT_METRIC);
  1564	    metrics.num_target_rows_inserted = get_metric(&target_count_metrics, TARGET_INSERTED_METRIC);
  1565	    metrics.num_target_rows_updated = get_metric(&target_count_metrics, TARGET_UPDATED_METRIC);
  1566	    metrics.num_target_rows_deleted = get_metric(&target_count_metrics, TARGET_DELETED_METRIC);
  1567	    metrics.num_target_rows_copied = get_metric(&target_count_metrics, TARGET_COPY_METRIC);
  1568	    metrics.num_output_rows = metrics.num_target_rows_inserted
  1569	        + metrics.num_target_rows_updated
  1570	        + metrics.num_target_rows_copied;
  1571	    let target_files_scanned_metric_names = [
  1572	        TARGET_FILES_SCANNED_METRIC,
  1573	        TARGET_FILES_SCANNED_METRIC_LEGACY,
  1574	    ];
  1575	    metrics.num_target_files_scanned = get_metric_any_or(
  1576	        &scan_count_metrics,
  1577	        &target_files_scanned_metric_names,
  1578	        || {
  1579	            warn!(
  1580	                %operation_id,
  1581	                metric_names = ?target_files_scanned_metric_names,
  1582	                "Missing target scan metric; defaulting target files scanned to zero"
  1583	            );
  1584	            0

  1728	    let impossible_state = scanned_files > total_files;
  1729	    (total_files.saturating_sub(scanned_files), impossible_state)

   240	impl Stream for MergeBarrierStream {
   241	    type Item = DataFusionResult<RecordBatch>;
   242	
   243	    fn poll_next(mut self: Pin<&mut Self>, cx: &mut Context<'_>) -> Poll<Option<Self::Item>> {
   244	        loop {
   245	            match self.state {
   246	                State::Feed => {
   247	                    match self.input.poll_next_unpin(cx) {
   248	                        Poll::Ready(Some(Ok(batch))) => {
   249	                            let file_dictionary = get_path_column(&batch, &self.file_column)?;
   250	
   251	                            // For each record batch, the key for a file path is not stable.
   252	                            // We can iterate through the dictionary and lookup the correspond string for each record and then lookup the correct `file_partition` for that value.
   253	                            // However this approach exposes the cost of hashing so we want to minimize that as much as possible.
   254	                            // A map from an arrow dictionary key to the correct index of `file_partition` is created for each batch that's processed.
   255	                            // This ensures we only need to hash each file path at most once per batch.
   256	                            let mut key_map = Vec::with_capacity(file_dictionary.len());
   257	
   258	                            for file_name in file_dictionary.values().into_iter() {
   259	                                let key = match file_name {
   260	                                    Some(name) => {
   261	                                        if !self.map.contains_key(name) {
   262	                                            let key = self.file_partitions.len();
   263	                                            let part_stream =
   264	                                                MergeBarrierPartition::new(Some(name.to_string()));
   265	                                            self.file_partitions.push(part_stream);
   266	                                            self.map.insert(name.to_string(), key);
   267	                                        }
   268	                                        // Safe unwrap due to the above
   269	                                        *self.map.get(name).unwrap()
   270	                                    }
   271	                                    None => 0,
   272	                                };
   273	                                key_map.push(key)
   274	                            }
   275	
   276	                            let mut indices: Vec<_> =
   277	                                Vec::with_capacity(self.file_partitions.len());
   278	                            for _ in 0..self.file_partitions.len() {
   279	                                indices.push(UInt64Builder::with_capacity(batch.num_rows()));
   280	                            }
   281	
   282	                            for (idx, key) in file_dictionary.keys().iter().enumerate() {
   283	                                match key {
   284	                                    Some(value) => {
   285	                                        indices[key_map[value as usize]].append_value(idx as u64)
   286	                                    }
   287	                                    None => indices[0].append_value(idx as u64),
   288	                                }
   289	                            }
   290	
   291	                            let batches: Vec<Result<(usize, RecordBatch), DataFusionError>> =
   292	                                indices
   293	                                    .into_iter()
   294	                                    .enumerate()
   295	                                    .filter_map(|(partition, mut indices)| {
   296	                                        let indices = indices.finish();
   297	                                        (!indices.is_empty()).then_some((partition, indices))
   298	                                    })
   299	                                    .map(move |(partition, indices)| {
   300	                                        // Produce batches based on indices
   301	                                        let columns = batch
   302	                                            .columns()
   303	                                            .iter()
   304	                                            .map(|c| {
   305	                                                Ok(arrow::compute::take(
   306	                                                    c.as_ref(),
   307	                                                    &indices,
   308	                                                    None,
   309	                                                )?)
   310	                                            })

     1	//! Merge Barrier determines which files have modifications during the merge operation
     2	//!
     3	//! For every unique path in the input stream, a barrier is established. If any
     4	//! single record for a file contains any delete, update, or insert operations
     5	//! then the barrier for the file is opened and can be sent downstream.
     6	//! To determine if a file contains zero changes, the input stream is
     7	//! exhausted. Afterwards, records are then dropped.
     8	//!
     9	//! Bookkeeping is maintained to determine which files have modifications, so
    10	//! they can be removed from the delta log.
    11	
    12	use std::{
    13	    collections::HashMap,
    14	    pin::Pin,
    15	    sync::Arc,
    16	    task::{Context, Poll},
    17	};
    18	
    19	use arrow::array::{Array, ArrayRef, RecordBatch, builder::UInt64Builder};
    20	use arrow::datatypes::SchemaRef;
    21	use dashmap::DashSet;
    22	use datafusion::common::{DataFusionError, Result as DataFusionResult};
    23	use datafusion::logical_expr::{Expr, LogicalPlan, UserDefinedLogicalNodeCore};
    24	use datafusion::physical_expr::{Distribution, PhysicalExpr};
    25	use datafusion::physical_plan::{
    26	    DisplayAs, DisplayFormatType, ExecutionPlan, RecordBatchStream, SendableRecordBatchStream,
    27	};
    28	use futures::{Stream, StreamExt};
    29	
    30	use crate::{
    31	    DeltaTableError,
    32	    delta_datafusion::get_path_column,
    33	    operations::merge::{TARGET_DELETE_COLUMN, TARGET_INSERT_COLUMN, TARGET_UPDATE_COLUMN},
    34	};
    35	
    36	pub(crate) type BarrierSurvivorSet = Arc<DashSet<String>>;
    37	
    38	#[derive(Debug)]
    39	/// Physical Node for the MergeBarrier
    40	/// Batches to this node must be repartitioned on col('deleta_rs_path').
    41	/// Each record batch then undergoes further partitioning based on the file column to it's corresponding barrier
    42	pub struct MergeBarrierExec {
    43	    input: Arc<dyn ExecutionPlan>,
    44	    file_column: Arc<String>,
    45	    survivors: BarrierSurvivorSet,
    46	    expr: Arc<dyn PhysicalExpr>,
    47	}
    48	
    49	impl MergeBarrierExec {
    50	    /// Create a new MergeBarrierExec Node
    51	    pub fn new(
    52	        input: Arc<dyn ExecutionPlan>,
    53	        file_column: Arc<String>,
    54	        expr: Arc<dyn PhysicalExpr>,
    55	    ) -> Self {
    56	        MergeBarrierExec {
    57	            input,
    58	            file_column,
    59	            survivors: Arc::new(DashSet::new()),
    60	            expr,
    61	        }
    62	    }
    63	
    64	    /// Files that have modifications to them and need to removed from the delta log
    65	    pub fn survivors(&self) -> BarrierSurvivorSet {
    66	        self.survivors.clone()
    67	    }
    68	}
    69	
    70	impl ExecutionPlan for MergeBarrierExec {
    71	    fn name(&self) -> &str {
    72	        Self::static_name()
    73	    }
    74	
    75	    fn as_any(&self) -> &dyn std::any::Any {
    76	        self
    77	    }
    78	
    79	    fn schema(&self) -> arrow_schema::SchemaRef {
    80	        self.input.schema()
    81	    }
    82	
    83	    fn properties(&self) -> &Arc<datafusion::physical_plan::PlanProperties> {
    84	        self.input.properties()
    85	    }
    86	
    87	    fn required_input_distribution(&self) -> Vec<Distribution> {
    88	        vec![Distribution::HashPartitioned(vec![self.expr.clone()]); 1]
    89	    }
    90	
    91	    fn children(&self) -> Vec<&Arc<dyn ExecutionPlan>> {
    92	        vec![&self.input]
    93	    }
    94	
    95	    fn with_new_children(
    96	        self: Arc<Self>,
    97	        children: Vec<Arc<dyn ExecutionPlan>>,
    98	    ) -> datafusion::common::Result<Arc<dyn ExecutionPlan>> {
    99	        if children.len() != 1 {
   100	            return Err(DataFusionError::Plan(
   101	                "MergeBarrierExec wrong number of children".to_string(),
   102	            ));
   103	        }
   104	        Ok(Arc::new(MergeBarrierExec::new(
   105	            children[0].clone(),
   106	            self.file_column.clone(),
   107	            self.expr.clone(),
   108	        )))
   109	    }
   110	
   111	    fn execute(
   112	        &self,
   113	        partition: usize,
   114	        context: Arc<datafusion::execution::TaskContext>,
   115	    ) -> datafusion::common::Result<datafusion::physical_plan::SendableRecordBatchStream> {
   116	        let input = self.input.execute(partition, context)?;
   117	        Ok(Box::pin(MergeBarrierStream::new(
   118	            input,
   119	            self.schema(),
   120	            self.survivors.clone(),
   121	            self.file_column.clone(),
   122	        )))
   123	    }
   124	}
   125	
   126	impl DisplayAs for MergeBarrierExec {
   127	    fn fmt_as(&self, t: DisplayFormatType, f: &mut std::fmt::Formatter) -> std::fmt::Result {
   128	        match t {
   129	            DisplayFormatType::Default
   130	            | DisplayFormatType::Verbose
   131	            | DisplayFormatType::TreeRender => {
   132	                write!(f, "MergeBarrier",)?;
   133	                Ok(())
   134	            }
   135	        }
   136	    }
   137	}
   138	
   139	#[derive(Debug)]
   140	enum State {
   141	    Feed,
   142	    Drain,
   143	    Finalize,
   144	    Abort,
   145	    Done,
   146	}
   147	
   148	#[derive(Debug)]
   149	enum PartitionBarrierState {
   150	    Closed,
   151	    Open,
   152	}
   153	
   154	#[derive(Debug)]
   155	struct MergeBarrierPartition {
   156	    state: PartitionBarrierState,
   157	    buffer: Vec<RecordBatch>,
   158	    file_name: Option<String>,
   159	}
   160	
   161	impl MergeBarrierPartition {
   162	    pub fn new(file_name: Option<String>) -> Self {
   163	        MergeBarrierPartition {
   164	            state: PartitionBarrierState::Closed,
   165	            buffer: Vec::new(),
   166	            file_name,
   167	        }
   168	    }
   169	
   170	    pub fn feed(&mut self, batch: RecordBatch) -> DataFusionResult<()> {
   171	        match self.state {
   172	            PartitionBarrierState::Closed => {
   173	                let delete_count = get_count(&batch, TARGET_DELETE_COLUMN)?;
   174	                let update_count = get_count(&batch, TARGET_UPDATE_COLUMN)?;
   175	                let insert_count = get_count(&batch, TARGET_INSERT_COLUMN)?;
   176	                self.buffer.push(batch);
   177	
   178	                if insert_count > 0 || update_count > 0 || delete_count > 0 {
   179	                    self.state = PartitionBarrierState::Open;
   180	                }
   181	            }
   182	            PartitionBarrierState::Open => {
   183	                self.buffer.push(batch);
   184	            }
   185	        }
   186	        Ok(())
   187	    }
   188	
   189	    pub fn drain(&mut self) -> Option<RecordBatch> {
   190	        match self.state {
   191	            PartitionBarrierState::Closed => None,
   192	            PartitionBarrierState::Open => self.buffer.pop(),
   193	        }
   194	    }
   195	}
   196	
   197	struct MergeBarrierStream {
   198	    schema: SchemaRef,
   199	    state: State,
   200	    input: SendableRecordBatchStream,
   201	    file_column: Arc<String>,
   202	    survivors: BarrierSurvivorSet,
   203	    map: HashMap<String, usize>,
   204	    file_partitions: Vec<MergeBarrierPartition>,
   205	}
   206	
   207	impl MergeBarrierStream {
   208	    pub fn new(
   209	        input: SendableRecordBatchStream,
   210	        schema: SchemaRef,
   211	        survivors: BarrierSurvivorSet,
   212	        file_column: Arc<String>,
   213	    ) -> Self {
   214	        // Always allocate for a null bucket at index 0;
   215	        let file_partitions = vec![MergeBarrierPartition::new(None)];
   216	
   217	        MergeBarrierStream {
   218	            schema,
   219	            state: State::Feed,
   220	            input,
   221	            file_column,
   222	            survivors,
   223	            file_partitions,
   224	            map: HashMap::new(),
   225	        }
   226	    }
   227	}
   228

   230	    batch

   104	    /// Create a selection from pre-normalized file IDs.
   105	    ///
   106	    /// This constructor does not normalize or validate the input IDs.
   107	    /// Callers with relative file paths or Add actions should prefer:
   108	    /// - [`FileSelection::from_file_paths`]
   109	    /// - [`FileSelection::from_adds`]
   110	    /// - [`normalize_path_as_file_id`]
   111	    pub(crate) fn new(file_ids: impl IntoIterator<Item = String>) -> Self {
   112	        Self {
   113	            file_ids: file_ids.into_iter().collect(),
   114	            missing_file_policy: MissingFilePolicy::Error,
   115	        }
   116	    }

   119	        self.missing_file_policy = policy;
   120	        self
   121	    }

   123	    pub(crate) fn from_file_paths(
   124	        file_paths: impl IntoIterator<Item = impl AsRef<str>>,
   125	        table_root_url: &Url,
   126	    ) -> crate::DeltaResult<Self> {
   127	        let table_root_url = ensure_table_root_url(table_root_url);
   128	        let mut file_ids = HashSet::new();

   141	        })
   142	    }

   152	pub(crate) fn ensure_table_root_url(table_root_url: &Url) -> Url {
   153	    if table_root_url.path().ends_with('/') {
   154	        table_root_url.clone()
   155	    } else {
   156	        let mut table_root_url = table_root_url.clone();
   157	        table_root_url.set_path(&format!("{}/", table_root_url.path()));
   158	        table_root_url
   159	    }
   160	}

   162	pub(crate) fn redact_url_for_error(url: &Url) -> String {
   163	    let mut redacted = url.clone();
   164	    let _ = redacted.set_password(None);
   165	    let _ = redacted.set_username("");
   166	    redacted.set_query(None);
   167	    redacted.set_fragment(None);
   168	    redacted.to_string()
   169	}
   170	
   171	pub(crate) fn redact_url_str_for_error(urlish: &str) -> String {
   172	    Url::parse(urlish).map_or_else(
   173	        |_| {
   174	            urlish
   175	                .split(['?', '#'])
   176	                .next()
   177	                .unwrap_or(urlish)
   178	                .to_string()
   179	        },
   180	        |url| redact_url_for_error(&url),
   181	    )
   182	}
   183	
   184	fn normalize_path_as_file_id_with_table_root(
   185	    path: &str,
   186	    table_root_url: &Url,
   187	    context: &'static str,
   188	) -> crate::DeltaResult<String> {
   189	    debug_assert!(
   190	        table_root_url.path().ends_with('/'),
   191	        "table_root_url must end with '/' before normalization"
   192	    );
   193	
   194	    let file_url = Url::parse(path)
   195	        .or_else(|_| table_root_url.join(path))
   196	        .map_err(|e| {
   197	            DeltaTableError::InvalidTableLocation(format!(
   198	                "Failed to normalize {context} '{}' against '{}': {e}",
   199	                redact_url_str_for_error(path),
   200	                redact_url_for_error(table_root_url),
   201	            ))
   202	        })?;
   203	
   204	    Ok(file_url.to_string())
   205	}
   206	
   207	pub(crate) fn normalize_path_as_file_id(
   208	    path: &str,
   209	    table_root_url: &Url,
   210	    context: &'static str,
   211	) -> crate::DeltaResult<String> {
   212	    let table_root_url = ensure_table_root_url(table_root_url);
   213	    normalize_path_as_file_id_with_table_root(path, &table_root_url, context)
   214	}
   215	
   216	#[derive(Clone, Debug, Serialize, Deserialize)]
   217	pub enum SnapshotWrapper {
   218	    Snapshot(Arc<Snapshot>),
   219	    EagerSnapshot(Arc<EagerSnapshot>),
   220	}
   221	
   222	impl From<Arc<Snapshot>> for SnapshotWrapper {
   223	    fn from(snap: Arc<Snapshot>) -> Self {
   224	        SnapshotWrapper::Snapshot(snap)
   225	    }

     2	
     3	use arrow_array::RecordBatch;
     4	use delta_kernel::actions::{Metadata, Protocol};
     5	use delta_kernel::expressions::{Scalar, StructData};

     9	
    10	use super::super::scalars::ScalarExt;
    11	use super::iterators::LogicalFileView;
    12	
    13	pub(crate) trait PartitionsExt {
    14	    fn hive_partition_path(&self) -> String;
    15	}
    16	
    17	impl PartitionsExt for IndexMap<String, Scalar> {
    18	    fn hive_partition_path(&self) -> String {
    19	        let sep = String::from('/');
    20	        itertools::Itertools::intersperse(
    21	            self.iter().map(|(k, v)| {
    22	                let encoded = v.serialize_encoded();
    23	                format!("{k}={encoded}")
    24	            }),
    25	            sep,
    26	        )
    27	        .collect()
    28	    }
    29	}
    30	
    31	impl PartitionsExt for StructData {
    32	    fn hive_partition_path(&self) -> String {
    33	        let sep = String::from('/');
    34	        itertools::Itertools::intersperse(
    35	            self.fields()
    36	                .iter()
    37	                .zip(self.values().iter())
    38	                .map(|(k, v)| {
    39	                    let encoded = v.serialize_encoded();
    40	                    format!("{}={encoded}", k.name())
    41	                }),
    42	            sep,
    43	        )
    44	        .collect()
    45	    }
    46	}
    47	
    48	impl<T: PartitionsExt> PartitionsExt for Arc<T> {
    49	    fn hive_partition_path(&self) -> String {
    50	        self.as_ref().hive_partition_path()
    51	    }
    52	}

    57	/// to avid the necessiity of knowing the exact layout of the underlying log data.
    58	#[derive(Clone)]
    59	pub struct LogDataHandler<'a> {
    60	    data: &'a [RecordBatch],
    61	    config: &'a TableConfiguration,
    62	}
    63	
    64	impl<'a> LogDataHandler<'a> {

    66	        Self { data, config }
    67	    }
    68

    70	        self.config
    71	    }
    72

     1	//! Internal synthetic file identifier utilities.
     2	//!
     3	//! `file_id` is an internal correlation mechanism used by the DataFusion integration to associate
     4	//! rows with their source file (e.g. per-file transforms, deletion vectors, and matched-file DML
     5	//! planning). It is intentionally centralized in this module to minimize schema/type drift.
     6	//!
     7	//! TODO(delta-io/delta-rs#4115): When ParquetAccessPlans can carry per-file transforms and DV
     8	//! filtering directly into the Parquet scan (and DV semantics become order-insensitive), this
     9	//! synthetic column should become unnecessary and can be removed.
    10	
    11	use std::sync::Arc;
    12	
    13	use arrow_schema::{DataType, Field, FieldRef};
    14	use datafusion::scalar::ScalarValue;
    15	use datafusion_datasource::file_scan_config::{
    16	    wrap_partition_type_in_dict, wrap_partition_value_in_dict,
    17	};
    18	
    19	/// Default column name for the synthetic file identifier.
    20	///
    21	/// This column is used internally to correlate rows back to their source file so we can apply
    22	/// per-file transforms (e.g. column mapping, deletion vectors) and to support DML rewrite scans.
    23	pub(crate) const FILE_ID_COLUMN_DEFAULT: &str = "__delta_rs_file_id__";
    24	
    25	/// Canonical Arrow type for the synthetic file-id column.
    26	///
    27	/// We keep this aligned with DataFusion's recommended dictionary encoding for partition values
    28	/// (`wrap_partition_type_in_dict`) so that both partition materialization and literal construction
    29	/// (`wrap_partition_value_in_dict`) agree on the dictionary key type (currently `UInt16`).
    30	///
    31	/// Note: we intentionally use `Utf8` (not `Utf8View`) because Arrow dictionary packing does not
    32	/// support view types.
    33	pub(crate) fn file_id_data_type() -> DataType {
    34	    wrap_partition_type_in_dict(DataType::Utf8)
    35	}
    36	
    37	/// Construct the canonical `file_id` field.
    38	pub(crate) fn file_id_field(name: Option<&str>) -> FieldRef {
    39	    Arc::new(Field::new(
    40	        name.unwrap_or(FILE_ID_COLUMN_DEFAULT),
    41	        file_id_data_type(),
    42	        false,
    43	    ))
    44	}
    45	
    46	/// Wrap a file path in the canonical dictionary encoding used for `file_id` values.
    47	pub(crate) fn wrap_file_id_value(path: impl Into<String>) -> ScalarValue {
    48	    wrap_partition_value_in_dict(ScalarValue::Utf8(Some(path.into())))
    49	}
    50

   526	fn split_by_file_id_runs(
   527	    batch: &RecordBatch,
   528	    file_id_idx: usize,
   529	) -> Result<Vec<(String, RecordBatch)>> {
   530	    if batch.num_rows() == 0 {
   531	        return Ok(Vec::new());
   532	    }
   533	
   534	    let dict = batch
   535	        .column(file_id_idx)
   536	        .as_any()
   537	        .downcast_ref::<arrow_array::DictionaryArray<UInt16Type>>()
   538	        .ok_or_else(|| {
   539	            internal_datafusion_err!(
   540	                "Expected file id column '{}' to be Dictionary<UInt16, Utf8|Utf8View>, got {:?}",
   541	                batch.schema_ref().field(file_id_idx).name(),
   542	                batch.column(file_id_idx).data_type()
   543	            )
   544	        })?;
   545	
   546	    // Parquet reads may yield Utf8 or Utf8View depending on DataFusion settings.
   547	    // Accept either for the synthetic file id column.
   548	    let keys = dict.keys();
   549	
   550	    enum FileIdValues<'a> {
   551	        Utf8(&'a StringArray),
   552	        Utf8View(&'a StringViewArray),
   553	    }
   554	
   555	    let values = if let Some(values) = dict
   556	        .values()
   557	        .as_ref()
   558	        .as_any()
   559	        .downcast_ref::<StringArray>()
   560	    {
   561	        FileIdValues::Utf8(values)
   562	    } else if let Some(values) = dict
   563	        .values()
   564	        .as_ref()
   565	        .as_any()
   566	        .downcast_ref::<StringViewArray>()
   567	    {
   568	        FileIdValues::Utf8View(values)
   569	    } else {
   570	        return Err(internal_datafusion_err!(
   571	            "Expected file id column '{}' to be Dictionary<UInt16, Utf8|Utf8View>, got {:?}",
   572	            batch.schema_ref().field(file_id_idx).name(),
   573	            batch.column(file_id_idx).data_type()
   574	        ));
   575	    };
   576	
   577	    let file_id_for_row = |row: usize| -> String {
   578	        let key = keys.value(row) as usize;
   579	        match values {
   580	            FileIdValues::Utf8(arr) => arr.value(key).to_string(),
   581	            FileIdValues::Utf8View(arr) => arr.value(key).to_string(),
   582	        }
   583	    };
   584	
   585	    if dict.is_null(0) {
   586	        return Err(internal_datafusion_err!("file id value must not be null"));
   587	    }
   588	
   589	    let mut prev_key = keys.value(0);
   590	    let mut start = 0usize;
   591	    let mut runs = Vec::new();
   592	
   593	    for i in 1..batch.num_rows() {
   594	        if dict.is_null(i) {
   595	            return Err(internal_datafusion_err!("file id value must not be null"));
   596	        }
   597	        let key = keys.value(i);
   598	        if key != prev_key {
   599	            let file_id = file_id_for_row(start);
   600	            runs.push((file_id, batch.slice(start, i - start)));
   601	            start = i;
   602	            prev_key = key;
   603	        }
   604	    }
   605	
   606	    let file_id = file_id_for_row(start);
   607	    runs.push((file_id, batch.slice(start, batch.num_rows() - start)));
   608	
   609	    Ok(runs)
   610	}

     1	//! Datafusion TableProvider implementation for Delta Lake tables.
     2	//!
     3	//! <div class="warning">
     4	//!
     5	//! The table provider is based on Snapshots of a Delta Table. Therefore, it represents
     6	//! a static view of the table at a specific point in time. Changes to the underlying
     7	//! Delta Table after the snapshot was taken will not be reflected in queries executed.
     8	//!
     9	//! To work with a dynamic view of the table that reflects ongoing changes, consider using
    10	//! the catalog abstractions in this crate, which provide a higher-level interface for managing
    11	//! Delta Tables within DataFusion sessions.
    12	//!
    13	//! </div>
    14	//!
    15	//! # Overview
    16	//!
    17	//! The [`DeltaScan`] struct integrates Delta Tables with DataFusion by implementing the
    18	//! `TableProvider` trait. It encapsulates all delta table-specific logic required to translate
    19	//! DataFusion's logical and physical plans into operations on Delta Lake data. This includes
    20	//! - table scans
    21	//!
    22	//! ## Table Scans
    23	//!
    24	//! Scanning a Delta Table involves two major steps:

    65	    where
    66	        S: Serializer,
    67	    {
    68	        let mut values: Vec<_> = set.iter().collect();
    69	        values.sort();

    71	    }

    74	    where
    75	        D: Deserializer<'de>,
    76	    {
    77	        let values = Vec::<String>::deserialize(deserializer)?;
    78	        Ok(values.into_iter().collect())
    79	    }

     1	//! Kernel-based Delta table scanning with optimized query execution.
     2	//!
     3	//! This module provides efficient table scanning using Delta Kernel, integrating with
     4	//! DataFusion's query engine. It supports:
     5	//!
     6	//! - **Physical scan execution** ([`DeltaScanExec`]) - Reads Parquet data files and applies
     7	//!   Delta protocol transformations (column mapping, deletion vectors, partition values)
     8	//! - **Metadata-only scans** ([`DeltaScanMetaExec`]) - Answers queries like `COUNT(*)`
     9	//!   using file statistics without reading data files
    10	//! - **Predicate pushdown** - Pushes filters to both kernel file skipping and Parquet readers
    11	//!   for efficient data pruning
    12	//! - **Multi-store support** - Handles files across different object stores in a single query
    13	//!
    14	//! The scan planning process in [`plan`] determines which files to read and how to apply
    15	//! predicates, while execution plans handle the actual data reading and transformation.

    76	pub(super) async fn execution_plan(

    78	    session: &dyn Session,

    80	    stream: ScanMetadataStream,

    83	    file_selection: Option<&FileSelection>,
    84	) -> Result<Arc<dyn ExecutionPlan>> {

    86	        replay_files(engine, &scan_plan, config.clone(), stream, file_selection).await?;
    87	
    88	    let file_id_field = config.file_id_field();
    89	    if scan_plan.is_metadata_only() {
    90	        let map_file = |f: &ScanFileContext| {
    91	            Ok((
    92	                f.file_url.to_string(),
    93	                match &f.stats.num_rows {
    94	                    Precision::Exact(n) => *n,
    95	                    _ => {
    96	                        return plan_err!(
    97	                            "Expected exact row counts in file: {}",
    98	                            super::redact_url_for_error(&f.file_url)
    99	                        );
   100	                    }
   101	                },
   102	            ))
   103	        };
   104	
   105	        let maybe_file_rows = files
   106	            .iter()
   107	            .map(map_file)
   108	            .try_collect::<_, VecDeque<_>, _>();
   109	        if let Ok(file_rows) = maybe_file_rows {
   110	            let exec = DeltaScanMetaExec::new(
   111	                Arc::new(scan_plan),
   112	                vec![file_rows],
   113	                Arc::new(transforms),
   114	                Arc::new(dvs),
   115	                config.retain_file_id().then_some(file_id_field),
   116	                metrics,
   117	            );
   118	            return Ok(Arc::new(exec) as _);
   119	        }
   120	    }
   121	
   122	    get_data_scan_plan(
   123	        session,
   124	        scan_plan,
   125	        files,
   126	        transforms,

   129	        limit,

   136	/// Materialize deletion vector keep masks for every file in the scan that has one.
   137	///
   138	/// Deletion vectors are loaded as a side-effect of consuming [`ScanFileStream`].  We drain the
   139	/// full stream here (discarding file contexts, stats, and partition values) because the DV
   140	/// loading tasks are spawned lazily during stream poll.  A dedicated DV-only stream that skips
   141	/// stats parsing is possible but not yet warranted — this path is not latency-sensitive and the
   142	/// file-list is typically small.
   143	///
   144	/// [`ReceiverStreamBuilder::build`] returns a merged stream that includes a JoinSet checker;
   145	/// `.try_collect().await` below will not complete until every spawned DV-loading task has
   146	/// finished, so no results are lost.
   147	pub(super) async fn replay_deletion_vectors(
   148	    engine: Arc<dyn Engine>,
   149	    scan_plan: &KernelScanPlan,
   150	    config: &DeltaScanConfig,
   151	    stream: ScanMetadataStream,
   152	) -> Result<Vec<DeletionVectorSelection>> {
   153	    let mut stream = ScanFileStream::new(engine, &scan_plan.scan, config.clone(), None, stream);
   154	    while stream.try_next().await?.is_some() {}
   155	
   156	    let dv_stream = stream.dv_stream.build();
   157	    // Only files with `dv_info.has_vector()` spawn tasks, so every item should carry a DV.
   158	    // Guard with a typed error (instead of panic) in case that invariant drifts.
   159	    let dvs: DashMap<_, _> = dv_stream
   160	        .and_then(|(url, dv, num_records)| {
   161	            ready(match dv {
   162	                Some(keep_mask) => normalize_dv_keep_mask_for_api(keep_mask, num_records, &url)
   163	                    .map(|mask| (url.to_string(), mask))
   164	                    .map_err(DeltaTableError::from),
   165	                None => Err(DeltaTableError::generic(
   166	                    "Invariant violation: DV task spawned for file without deletion vector",
   167	                )),
   168	            })
   169	        })
   170	        .try_collect()
   171	        .await?;
   172	
   173	    let mut vectors: Vec<_> = dvs
   174	        .into_iter()
   175	        .map(|(filepath, keep_mask)| DeletionVectorSelection {
   176	            filepath,
   177	            keep_mask,
   178	        })
   179	        .collect();
   180	    vectors.sort_unstable_by(|left, right| left.filepath.cmp(&right.filepath));
   181	    Ok(vectors)
   182	}
   183	
   184	async fn replay_files(
   185	    engine: Arc<dyn Engine>,
   186	    scan_plan: &KernelScanPlan,
   187	    scan_config: DeltaScanConfig,
   188	    stream: ScanMetadataStream,
   189	    file_selection: Option<&FileSelection>,
   190	) -> Result<(
   191	    Vec<ScanFileContext>,
   192	    HashMap<String, Arc<Expression>>,
   193	    DashMap<String, Vec<bool>>,
   194	    ExecutionPlanMetricsSet,
   195	)> {
   196	    let mut stream = ScanFileStream::new(
   197	        engine,
   198	        &scan_plan.scan,
   199	        scan_config,
   200	        file_selection.map(|selection| &selection.file_ids),
   201	        stream,
   202	    );
   203	    let mut files = Vec::new();
   204	    while let Some(file) = stream.try_next().await? {
   205	        files.extend(file);
   206	    }
   207	
   208	    if let Some(selection) = file_selection
   209	        && selection.missing_file_policy == super::MissingFilePolicy::Error
   210	    {
   211	        let found: std::collections::HashSet<_> =
   212	            files.iter().map(|f| f.file_url.to_string()).collect();
   213	        let all_missing: Vec<_> = selection.file_ids.difference(&found).sorted().collect();
   214	
   215	        if !all_missing.is_empty() {
   216	            let missing_total = all_missing.len();
   217	            let missing: Vec<_> = all_missing
   218	                .iter()
   219	                .take(10)
   220	                .map(|id| super::redact_url_str_for_error(id))
   221	                .collect();
   222	            let extra = if missing_total > missing.len() {
   223	                format!(" (and {} more)", missing_total - missing.len())
   224	            } else {
   225	                String::new()
   226	            };
   227	            return plan_err!(
   228	                "File selection contains {missing_total} missing files (showing up to 10, redacted): {}{extra}",
   229	                missing.join(", ")
   230	            );
   231	        }
   232	    }
   233	
   234	    let transforms: HashMap<_, _> = files
   235	        .iter_mut()
   236	        .flat_map(|file| {
   237	            file.transform
   238	                .take()
   239	                .map(|t| (file.file_url.to_string(), t))
   240	        })
   241	        .collect();
   242	
   243	    let dv_stream = stream.dv_stream.build();
   244	    let dvs: DashMap<_, _> = dv_stream
   245	        .try_filter_map(|(url, dv, _)| ready(Ok(dv.map(|dv| (url.to_string(), dv)))))
   246	        .try_collect()
   247	        .await?;
   248	
   249	    let metrics = ExecutionPlanMetricsSet::new();
   250	    MetricBuilder::new(&metrics)
   251	        .global_counter("count_files_scanned")
   252	        .add(stream.metrics.num_scanned);
   253	
   254	    Ok((files, transforms, dvs, metrics))
   255	}
   256	
   257	/// Normalize a DV keep mask for `deletion_vectors()`.
   258	///
   259	/// Kernel returns a sparse mask (up to the highest deleted row index). For API output we need one
   260	/// full mask per file, to do this we pad trailing entries with `true` up to `numRecords`. If `numRecords`
   261	/// is missing we fail, because we cannot know the correct full length.
   262	///
   263	/// This is API only. Scan execution does per batch normalization in `exec::consume_dv_mask` and
   264	/// `exec_meta::apply_selection_vector`.
   265	fn normalize_dv_keep_mask_for_api(
   266	    mut mask: Vec<bool>,
   267	    num_records: Option<u64>,
   268	    file_url: &Url,
   269	) -> Result<Vec<bool>> {
   270	    let redacted_url = super::redact_url_for_error(file_url);

    59	/// Extracts column names referenced in the scan's physical predicate.
    60	///
    61	/// Returns a set of column names that are actually used in predicates, which helps
    62	/// optimize statistics parsing to only process relevant columns.
    63	fn extract_predicate_columns(scan: &KernelScan) -> Option<HashSet<String>> {
    64	    scan.physical_predicate().map(|predicate| {
    65	        predicate
    66	            .references()
    67	            .into_iter()
    68	            .map(|col_name| col_name.to_string().trim_matches('`').to_string())
    69	            .collect()
    70	    })
    71	}
    72	
    73	/// Create a stats schema containing only columns needed for predicate evaluation
    74	///
    75	/// Returns:
    76	/// - If no predicate: Schema with just `numRecords`
    77	/// - If predicate exists: Schema with `numRecords` + stats for referenced columns only
    78	fn create_minimal_stats_schema(
    79	    scan: &KernelScan,
    80	    predicate_columns: Option<&HashSet<String>>,
    81	) -> DeltaResult<Arc<Schema>> {
    82	    let minimal_schema = || {
    83	        Schema::try_new(vec![StructField::nullable("numRecords", DataType::LONG)])
    84	            .map(Arc::new)
    85	            .map_err(Into::into)
    86	    };
    87	
    88	    match predicate_columns {
    89	        None => {
    90	            // No predicate - only need numRecords for file statistics
    91	            minimal_schema()
    92	        }
    93	        Some(cols) if cols.is_empty() => {
    94	            // Empty predicate columns - minimal schema
    95	            minimal_schema()
    96	        }
    97	        Some(cols) => {
    98	            // Filter physical schema to only referenced columns
    99	            let physical_schema = scan.physical_schema();
   100	            let filtered_fields: Vec<_> = physical_schema
   101	                .fields()
   102	                .filter(|field| cols.contains(field.name()))
   103	                .cloned()
   104	                .collect();
   105	
   106	            if filtered_fields.is_empty() {
   107	                // Predicate references only partition columns - minimal schema
   108	                minimal_schema()
   109	            } else {
   110	                // Create stats schema for filtered fields
   111	                let filtered_schema = Schema::try_new(filtered_fields)?;
   112	                Ok(Arc::new(stats_schema(
   113	                    &filtered_schema,
   114	                    scan.snapshot().table_properties(),
   115	                )))
   116	            }
   117	        }
   118	    }
   119	}

   122	    /// Stream that processes kernel scan metadata into file contexts with statistics.
   123	    ///
   124	    /// This stream consumes [`ScanMetadata`] from Delta Kernel's scan and produces
   125	    /// [`ScanFileContext`] entries enriched with:
   126	    ///
   127	    /// - **File statistics**: Row counts, min/max values, null counts
   128	    /// - **Deletion vectors**: Asynchronously loaded and cached
   129	    /// - **Partition values**: Extracted from file metadata
   130	    /// - **Transforms**: Column mapping expressions for physical-to-logical translation
   131	    pub(crate) struct ScanFileStream<'a, S> {
   132	        pub(crate) metrics: ReplayStats,
   133	
   134	        engine: Arc<dyn Engine>,
   135	
   136	        table_root: Url,
   137	
   138	        kernel_scan: Arc<KernelScan>,
   139	
   140	        scan_config: DeltaScanConfig,
   141	
   142	        file_selection: Option<&'a HashSet<String>>,
   143	
   144	        pub(crate) dv_stream: ReceiverStreamBuilder<(Url, Option<Vec<bool>>, Option<u64>)>,
   145	
   146	        #[pin]
   147	        stream: S,
   148	    }
   149	}
   150	
   151	impl<'a, S> ScanFileStream<'a, S> {
   152	    pub(crate) fn new(
   153	        engine: Arc<dyn Engine>,
   154	        scan: &Arc<Scan>,
   155	        scan_config: DeltaScanConfig,
   156	        file_selection: Option<&'a HashSet<String>>,
   157	        stream: S,
   158	    ) -> Self {
   159	        Self {
   160	            metrics: ReplayStats::new(),
   161	            dv_stream: ReceiverStreamBuilder::<(Url, Option<Vec<bool>>, Option<u64>)>::new(100),
   162	            engine,
   163	            table_root: scan.table_root().clone(),
   164	            kernel_scan: scan.inner().clone(),
   165	            stream,
   166	            scan_config,
   167	            file_selection,
   168	        }
   169	    }
   170	}

   172	impl<'a, S> Stream for ScanFileStream<'a, S>
   173	where
   174	    S: Stream<Item = DeltaResult<ScanMetadata>>,
   175	{
   176	    type Item = DeltaResult<Vec<ScanFileContext>>;
   177	
   178	    fn poll_next(self: Pin<&mut Self>, cx: &mut Context<'_>) -> Poll<Option<Self::Item>> {
   179	        let this = self.project();
   180	        let physical_arrow = this
   181	            .kernel_scan
   182	            .physical_schema()
   183	            .as_ref()
   184	            .try_into_arrow()
   185	            .unwrap();
   186	        match this.stream.poll_next(cx) {
   187	            Poll::Ready(Some(Ok(scan_data))) => {
   188	                let scan_data = if let Some(selection) = this.file_selection {
   189	                    match apply_file_selection(scan_data, this.table_root, selection) {
   190	                        Ok(scan_data) => scan_data,
   191	                        Err(err) => return Poll::Ready(Some(Err(err))),
   192	                    }
   193	                } else {
   194	                    scan_data
   195	                };
   196	
   197	                let ctx = match scan_data
   198	                    .visit_scan_files(ScanContext::new(this.table_root.clone()), visit_scan_file)
   199	                    .map_err(|err| DataFusionError::from(DeltaTableError::from(err)))
   200	                    .and_then(ScanContext::error_or)
   201	                {
   202	                    Ok(ctx) => ctx,
   203	                    Err(err) => return Poll::Ready(Some(Err(err.into()))),
   204	                };
   205	
   206	                // Spawn tasks to read the deletion vectors from disk.
   207	                for file in &ctx.files {
   208	                    if file.dv_info.has_vector() {
   209	                        let engine = this.engine.clone();
   210	                        let dv_info = file.dv_info.clone();
   211	                        let file_url = file.file_url.clone();
   212	                        let num_records = file.num_records;
   213	                        let table_root = this.table_root.clone();
   214	                        let tx = this.dv_stream.tx();
   215	
   216	                        let load_dv = move || {
   217	                            let dv = dv_info.get_selection_vector(engine.as_ref(), &table_root)?;
   218	                            let _ = tx.blocking_send(Ok((file_url, dv, num_records)));
   219	                            Ok(())
   220	                        };

   280	/// Extracts DataFusion statistics from parsed file metadata.
   281	///
   282	/// Converts Delta Kernel's file statistics into DataFusion's [`Statistics`] format,
   283	/// which is used for query optimization and predicate pushdown. This function implements
   284	/// an important optimization: it only extracts statistics for columns that appear in
   285	/// predicates, avoiding expensive parsing for unused columns.
   286	///
   287	/// # Arguments
   288	///
   289	/// * `scan` - The kernel scan containing schema and predicate information
   290	/// * `parsed_stats` - RecordBatch containing parsed statistics for all files
   291	/// * `predicate_columns` - Optional set of columns referenced in predicates
   292	///
   293	/// # Returns
   294	///
   295	/// A map from file URL to tuple of:
   296	/// - [`Statistics`]: DataFusion statistics for query optimization
   297	/// - [`StructData`]: Partition values to be materialized in the output
   298	fn extract_file_statistics(
   299	    scan: &KernelScan,
   300	    scan_config: &DeltaScanConfig,
   301	    parsed_stats: RecordBatch,
   302	    predicate_columns: Option<&HashSet<String>>,
   303	) -> HashMap<Url, (Statistics, Option<StructData>)> {
   304	    (0..parsed_stats.num_rows())
   305	        .map(move |idx| LogicalFileView::new(parsed_stats.clone(), idx))
   306	        .filter_map(|view| {
   307	            let num_rows = view
   308	                .num_records()
   309	                .map(Precision::Exact)
   310	                .unwrap_or(Precision::Absent);
   311	            let total_byte_size = Precision::Exact(view.size() as usize);
   312	
   313	            let null_counts = extract_struct(view.null_counts());
   314	            let max_values = extract_struct(view.max_values());
   315	            let min_values = extract_struct(view.min_values());
   316	
   317	            let column_statistics = scan
   318	                .physical_schema()
   319	                .fields()
   320	                .map(|f| {
   321	                    // Check if we should extract stats for this column
   322	                    let should_extract_stats = predicate_columns
   323	                        .map(|cols| cols.contains(f.name()))
   324	                        .unwrap_or(false); // No predicate = no stats needed for pruning
   325	
   326	                    if !should_extract_stats {
   327	                        // Return unknown statistics for non-predicate columns
   328	                        return ColumnStatistics {
   329	                            null_count: Precision::Absent,
   330	                            max_value: Precision::Absent,
   331	                            min_value: Precision::Absent,
   332	                            sum_value: Precision::Absent,
   333	                            distinct_count: Precision::Absent,
   334	                            byte_size: Precision::Absent,
   335	                        };
   336	                    }
   337	
   338	                    // Extract statistics for predicate columns
   339	                    let null_count = if let Some(field_index) =
   340	                        null_counts.as_ref().and_then(|v| v.index_of(f.name()))
   341	                    {
   342	                        null_counts
   343	                            .as_ref()
   344	                            .map(|v| match v.values()[field_index] {
   345	                                Scalar::Integer(int_val) => Precision::Exact(int_val as usize),
   346	                                Scalar::Long(long_val) => Precision::Exact(long_val as usize),
   347	                                _ => Precision::Absent,
   348	                            })
   349	                            .unwrap_or_default()
   350	                    } else {
   351	                        Precision::Absent
   352	                    };
   353	
   354	                    let max_value =
   355	                        physical_precision(extract_precision(&max_values, f.name()), scan_config);
   356	                    let min_value =
   357	                        physical_precision(extract_precision(&min_values, f.name()), scan_config);
   358	
   359	                    ColumnStatistics {
   360	                        null_count,
   361	                        max_value,
   362	                        min_value,
   363	                        sum_value: Precision::Absent,
   364	                        distinct_count: Precision::Absent,
   365	                        byte_size: Precision::Absent,
   366	                    }
   367	                })
   368	                .collect_vec();
   369	
   370	            Some((
   371	                parse_path(scan.snapshot().table_root(), view.path_raw()).ok()?,
   372	                (
   373	                    Statistics {
   374	                        num_rows,
   375	                        total_byte_size,
   376	                        column_statistics,
   377	                    },
   378	                    view.partition_values(),
   379	                ),
   380	            ))
   381	        })
   382	        .collect()
   383	}
   384	
   385	#[inline]
   386	fn physical_precision(
   387	    precision: Precision<ScalarValue>,
   388	    scan_config: &DeltaScanConfig,
   389	) -> Precision<ScalarValue> {
   390	    match precision {
   391	        Precision::Exact(v) => Precision::Exact(scan_config.map_scalar_value(v)),
   392	        Precision::Inexact(v) => Precision::Inexact(scan_config.map_scalar_value(v)),
   393	        Precision::Absent => Precision::Absent,
   394	    }
   395	}
   396	
   397	fn extract_precision(data: &Option<StructData>, name: impl AsRef<str>) -> Precision<ScalarValue> {
   398	    if let Some(field_index) = data.as_ref().and_then(|v| v.index_of(name.as_ref())) {
   399	        data.as_ref()
   400	            .map(|v| match to_datafusion_scalar(&v.values()[field_index]) {
   401	                Ok(df) => Precision::Exact(df),
   402	                _ => Precision::Absent,
   403	            })
   404	            .unwrap_or_default()
   405	    } else {
   406	        Precision::Absent
   407	    }
   408	}
   409	
   410	fn extract_struct(scalar: Option<Scalar>) -> Option<StructData> {
   411	    match scalar {
   412	        Some(Scalar::Struct(data)) => Some(data),
   413	        _ => None,
   414	    }
   415	}
   416	
   417	/// Enriched metadata for a single data file in a table scan.
   418	///
   419	/// Contains all information needed by DataFusion to read and process a Parquet file
   420	/// as part of a Delta table scan. This includes the file location, size, statistics,
   421	/// and any transformations required by the Delta protocol.
   422	///
   423	/// # Fields
   424	///
   425	/// - [`file_url`](Self::file_url): Complete URL for reading the file from object storage
   426	/// - [`size`](Self::size): File size in bytes for I/O planning
   427	/// - [`transform`](Self::transform): Expression to apply partition values and column mapping
   428	/// - [`stats`](Self::stats): File-level statistics for predicate pushdown and pruning
   429	/// - [`partitions`](Self::partitions): Partition column values to materialize
   430	///
   431	/// These contexts are created during the scan replay phase and consumed by execution plans.
   432	#[derive(Debug)]
   433	pub(crate) struct ScanFileContext {
   434	    /// Fully qualified URL of the file.
   435	    pub file_url: Url,
   436	    /// Size of the file on disk.
   437	    pub size: u64,
   438	    /// Transformations to apply to the data in the file.

   461	/// Metadata to read a data file from object storage.
   462	struct ScanFileContextInner {
   463	    /// Fully qualified URL of the file.
   464	    pub file_url: Url,
   465	    /// Size of the file on disk.
   466	    pub size: u64,
   467	    /// Transformations to apply to the data in the file.
   468	    pub transform: Option<ExpressionRef>,

   470	    pub num_records: Option<u64>,
   471

   473	}
   474	
   475	struct ScanContext {
   476	    /// Table root URL
   477	    table_root: Url,
   478	    /// Files to be scanned.
   479	    files: Vec<ScanFileContextInner>,
   480	    /// Errors encountered during the scan.
   481	    errs: DataFusionErrorBuilder,
   482	    count: usize,
   483	}
   484	
   485	impl ScanContext {
   486	    fn new(table_root: Url) -> Self {
   487	        Self {
   488	            table_root,
   489	            files: Vec::new(),
   490	            errs: DataFusionErrorBuilder::new(),
   491	            count: 0,
   492	        }
   493	    }
   494	
   495	    fn parse_path(&self, path: &str) -> DeltaResult<Url, DataFusionError> {
   496	        parse_path(&self.table_root, path)
   497	    }
   498	
   499	    fn error_or(self) -> DeltaResult<Self, DataFusionError> {
   500	        let ScanContext {
   501	            table_root,
   502	            files,
   503	            errs,
   504	            count,
   505	        } = self;
   506	        errs.error_or(())?;
   507	        Ok(ScanContext {
   508	            table_root,
   509	            files,
   510	            errs: DataFusionErrorBuilder::new(),
   511	            count,
   512	        })
   513	    }
   514	}
   515	
   516	fn parse_path(url: &Url, path: &str) -> DeltaResult<Url, DataFusionError> {
   517	    Ok(match Url::parse(path) {
   518	        Ok(url) => url,
   519	        Err(_) => url
   520	            .join(path)
   521	            .map_err(|e| DataFusionError::External(Box::new(e)))?,
   522	    })
   523	}
   524	
   525	fn apply_file_selection(
   526	    mut scan_data: ScanMetadata,
   527	    table_root: &Url,
   528	    file_selection: &HashSet<String>,
   529	) -> DeltaResult<ScanMetadata> {
   530	    let (data, mut selection_vector) = scan_data.scan_files.into_parts();
   531	    let batch: RecordBatch = ArrowEngineData::try_from_engine_data(data)?.into();
   532	
   533	    // Kernel allows a shorter selection vector; missing entries are implicitly true.
   534	    selection_vector.resize(batch.num_rows(), true);
   535	
   536	    for (idx, select) in selection_vector.iter_mut().enumerate() {
   537	        if *select {
   538	            let file_url = parse_path(
   539	                table_root,
   540	                LogicalFileView::new(batch.clone(), idx).path_raw(),
   541	            )?;
   542	            *select = file_selection.contains(file_url.as_str());
   543	        }
   544	    }
   545	
   546	    scan_data.scan_files =
   547	        FilteredEngineData::try_new(Box::new(ArrowEngineData::new(batch)), selection_vector)?;
   548	    Ok(scan_data)
   549	}
   550	
   551	fn visit_scan_file(ctx: &mut ScanContext, scan_file: ScanFile) {
   552	    let file_url = match ctx.parse_path(&scan_file.path) {
   553	        Ok(v) => v,
   554	        Err(e) => {
   555	            ctx.errs.add_error(e);
   556	            return;
   557	        }
   558	    };
   559	
   560	    ctx.files.push(ScanFileContextInner {
   561	        dv_info: scan_file.dv_info,
   562	        transform: scan_file.transform,
   563	        file_url,
   564	        size: scan_file.size as u64,
   565	        num_records: scan_file.stats.map(|stats| stats.num_records),
   566	    });
   567	    ctx.count += 1;
   568	}

   300	    metrics: ExecutionPlanMetricsSet,
   301	    limit: Option<usize>,
   302	    file_id_field: FieldRef,
   303	    retain_file_ids: bool,
   304	) -> Result<Arc<dyn ExecutionPlan>> {
   305	    let mut partition_stats = HashMap::new();
   306	
   307	    // Convert the files into datafusions `PartitionedFile`s grouped by the object store they are stored in
   308	    // this is used to create a DataSourceExec plan for each store
   309	    // To correlate the data with the original file, we add the file url as a partition value
   310	    // This is required to apply the correct transform to the data in downstream processing.
   311	    let to_partitioned_file = |f: ScanFileContext| {
   312	        if let Some(part_stata) = &f.partitions {
   313	            update_partition_stats(part_stata, &f.stats, &mut partition_stats)?;
   314	        }
   315	        // We create a PartitionedFile from the ObjectMeta to avoid any surprises in path encoding
   316	        // that may arise from using the 'new' method directly. i.e. the 'new' method encodes paths
   317	        // segments again, which may lead to double-encoding in some cases.
   318	        let mut partitioned_file: PartitionedFile = ObjectMeta {
   319	            location: Path::from_url_path(f.file_url.path())?,
   320	            size: f.size,
   321	            last_modified: Utc.timestamp_nanos(0),
   322	            e_tag: None,
   323	            version: None,
   324	        }
   325	        .into();
   326	        let file_value = wrap_file_id_value(f.file_url.as_str());
   327	        // NOTE: `PartitionedFile::with_statistics` appends exact stats for partition columns based
   328	        // on `partition_values`, so partition values must be set first.
   329	        partitioned_file.partition_values = vec![file_value.clone()];
   330	        partitioned_file = partitioned_file.with_statistics(Arc::new(f.stats));

   260	        .collect::<Vec<_>>();
   261	    Arc::new(ArrowSchema::new(fields))
   262	}
   263	
   264	pub(crate) fn files_matching_predicate<'a>(
   265	    log_data: LogDataHandler<'a>,
   266	    filters: &[Expr],
   267	) -> DeltaResult<impl Iterator<Item = Add> + 'a> {
   268	    if let Some(Some(predicate)) =
   269	        (!filters.is_empty()).then_some(conjunction(filters.iter().cloned()))
   270	    {
   271	        let expr = SessionContext::new()
   272	            .create_physical_expr(predicate, &log_data.read_schema().to_dfschema()?)?;
   273	        let pruning_predicate = PruningPredicate::try_new(expr, log_data.read_schema())?;
   274	        let mask = pruning_predicate.prune(&log_data)?;
   275	
   276	        Ok(Either::Left(log_data.into_iter().zip(mask).filter_map(
   277	            |(file, keep_file)| {
   278	                if keep_file { Some(file.to_add()) } else { None }
   279	            },
   280	        )))
   281	    } else {
   282	        Ok(Either::Right(
   283	            log_data.into_iter().map(|file| file.to_add()),
   284	        ))
   285	    }
   286	}
   287	
   288	pub(crate) fn get_path_column<'a>(
   289	    batch: &'a RecordBatch,
   290	    path_column: &str,
   291	) -> DeltaResult<TypedDictionaryArray<'a, UInt16Type, StringArray>> {
   292	    let err = || DeltaTableError::Generic("Unable to obtain Delta-rs path column".to_string());
   293	    batch
   294	        .column_by_name(path_column)
   295	        .unwrap()
   296	        .as_any()
   297	        .downcast_ref::<DictionaryArray<UInt16Type>>()
   298	        .ok_or_else(err)?
   299	        .downcast_dict::<StringArray>()
   300	        .ok_or_else(err)
   301	}
   302	
   303	pub(crate) fn get_null_of_arrow_type(t: &ArrowDataType) -> DeltaResult<ScalarValue> {
   304	    match t {
   305	        ArrowDataType::Null => Ok(ScalarValue::Null),
   306	        ArrowDataType::Boolean => Ok(ScalarValue::Boolean(None)),
   307	        ArrowDataType::Int8 => Ok(ScalarValue::Int8(None)),
   308	        ArrowDataType::Int16 => Ok(ScalarValue::Int16(None)),
   309	        ArrowDataType::Int32 => Ok(ScalarValue::Int32(None)),
   310	        ArrowDataType::Int64 => Ok(ScalarValue::Int64(None)),
   311	        ArrowDataType::UInt8 => Ok(ScalarValue::UInt8(None)),
   312	        ArrowDataType::UInt16 => Ok(ScalarValue::UInt16(None)),
   313	        ArrowDataType::UInt32 => Ok(ScalarValue::UInt32(None)),
   314	        ArrowDataType::UInt64 => Ok(ScalarValue::UInt64(None)),
   315	        ArrowDataType::Float32 => Ok(ScalarValue::Float32(None)),
   316	        ArrowDataType::Float64 => Ok(ScalarValue::Float64(None)),
   317	        ArrowDataType::Date32 => Ok(ScalarValue::Date32(None)),
   318	        ArrowDataType::Date64 => Ok(ScalarValue::Date64(None)),
   319	        ArrowDataType::Binary => Ok(ScalarValue::Binary(None)),
   320	        ArrowDataType::FixedSizeBinary(size) => {
   321	            Ok(ScalarValue::FixedSizeBinary(size.to_owned(), None))
   322	        }
   323	        ArrowDataType::LargeBinary => Ok(ScalarValue::LargeBinary(None)),
   324	        ArrowDataType::Utf8 => Ok(ScalarValue::Utf8(None)),
   325	        ArrowDataType::LargeUtf8 => Ok(ScalarValue::LargeUtf8(None)),
   326	        ArrowDataType::Decimal128(precision, scale) => Ok(ScalarValue::Decimal128(
   327	            None,
   328	            precision.to_owned(),
   329	            scale.to_owned(),
   330	        )),

    18	async fn create_table(table_uri: &str, partition: Option<Vec<&str>>) -> DeltaTable {
    19	    let table_schema = get_delta_schema();
    20	    let table_url = url::Url::from_directory_path(table_uri).unwrap();
    21	    let ops = DeltaTable::try_from_url(table_url).await.unwrap();
    22	    let table = ops
    23	        .create()
    24	        .with_columns(table_schema.fields().cloned())
    25	        .with_partition_columns(partition.unwrap_or_default())
    26	        .await
    27	        .expect("Failed to create table");
    28	
    29	    let schema = get_arrow_schema();
    30	    write_data(table, &schema).await
    31	}

   117	async fn merge(
   118	    table: DeltaTable,
   119	    df: DataFrame,
   120	    predicate: Expr,
   121	) -> DeltaResult<(DeltaTable, MergeMetrics)> {
   122	    table
   123	        .merge(df, predicate)
   124	        .with_source_alias("source")
   125	        .with_target_alias("target")
   126	        .when_matched_update(|update| {
   127	            update
   128	                .update("value", col("source.value"))
   129	                .update("event_date", col("source.event_date"))
   130	        })
   131	        .unwrap()
   132	        .when_not_matched_insert(|insert| {
   133	            insert
   134	                .set("id", col("source.id"))
   135	                .set("value", col("source.value"))
   136	                .set("event_date", col("source.event_date"))
   137	        })
   138	        .unwrap()
   139	        .await
   140	}

        return Ok(true);
    }

    // Compare against normalized file IDs.
    let full_id = normalize_path_as_file_id(rel_path, table_root, "merge remove")?;
    if survivors.contains(full_id.as_str()) {
        return Ok(true);
    }

    // DataFusion/object-store paths may be materialized with URL escapes decoded
    // (for example, a partition directory `group=foo%20bar` can appear in the
    // file-id column as `group=foo bar`). Normalize the internally collected
    // survivor IDs before comparing so rewritten files are removed regardless
    // of whether their partition path segments are escaped or decoded.
    Ok(survivors.iter().any(|survivor| {
        normalize_path_as_file_id(survivor.as_str(), table_root, "merge survivor")
            .is_ok_and(|survivor_id| survivor_id == full_id)
    }))
}
'

  1491	/// Convert type to a type suitable for use as a `ListingTable`
  1492	/// partition column. Returns `Dictionary(UInt16, val_type)`, which is
  1493	/// a reasonable trade off between a reasonable number of partition
  1494	/// values and space efficiency.
  1495	///
  1496	/// This use this to specify types for partition columns. However
  1497	/// you MAY also choose not to dictionary-encode the data or to use a
  1498	/// different dictionary type.
  1499	///
  1500	/// Use [`wrap_partition_value_in_dict`] to wrap a [`ScalarValue`] in the same say.
  1501	pub fn wrap_partition_type_in_dict(val_type: DataType) -> DataType {
  1502	    DataType::Dictionary(Box::new(DataType::UInt16), Box::new(val_type))
  1503	}
  1504	
  1505	/// Convert a [`ScalarValue`] of partition columns to a type, as
  1506	/// described in the documentation of [`wrap_partition_type_in_dict`],
  1507	/// which can wrap the types.
  1508	pub fn wrap_partition_value_in_dict(val: ScalarValue) -> ScalarValue {
  1509	    ScalarValue::Dictionary(Box::new(DataType::UInt16), Box::new(val))
  1510	}

[package]
name = "repro_merge_space"

[dependencies]

cat > /tmp/repro_merge_space/src/main.rs <<'RS'
use std::sync::Arc;
use arrow_array::{RecordBatch, StringArray, Int32Array};
use arrow_schema::{DataType, Field, Schema};
use datafusion::prelude::*;
use deltalake_core::{DeltaTable, DeltaResult};
use deltalake_core::kernel::{StructType, StructField, DataType as DeltaDataType, PrimitiveType};

fn delta_schema() -> StructType {
    StructType::try_new(vec![
        StructField::new("group".into(), DeltaDataType::Primitive(PrimitiveType::String), true),
        StructField::new("region".into(), DeltaDataType::Primitive(PrimitiveType::String), true),
        StructField::new("val".into(), DeltaDataType::Primitive(PrimitiveType::Integer), true),
    ]).unwrap()
}

fn arrow_schema() -> Arc<Schema> {
    Arc::new(Schema::new(vec![
        Field::new("group", DataType::Utf8, true),
        Field::new("region", DataType::Utf8, true),
        Field::new("val", DataType::Int32, true),
    ]))
}

fn source(ctx: &SessionContext, group: &str) -> datafusion::error::Result<DataFrame> {
    let schema = arrow_schema();
    let batch = RecordBatch::try_new(schema, vec![
        Arc::new(StringArray::from(vec![group, group, group])),
        Arc::new(StringArray::from(vec!["A", "B", "C"])),
        Arc::new(Int32Array::from(vec![1, 2, 3])),
    ])?;
    ctx.read_batch(batch)
}

async fn run(group: &str) -> DeltaResult<()> {
    let dir = tempfile::tempdir().unwrap();
    let table_url = url::Url::from_directory_path(dir.path()).unwrap();
    let ops = DeltaTable::try_from_url(table_url).await.unwrap();
    let mut table = ops.create()
        .with_columns(delta_schema().fields().cloned())
        .with_partition_columns(vec!["group"])
        .await?;

    for i in 1..=2 {
        let ctx = SessionContext::new();
        let source = source(&ctx, group).unwrap();
        let predicate = col("target.group").eq(lit(group))
            .and(col("target.region").eq(col("source.region")));
        let (new_table, metrics) = table.merge(source, predicate)
            .with_source_alias("source")
            .with_target_alias("target")
            .when_matched_update(|u| u.update("val", col("source.val"))).unwrap()
            .when_not_matched_insert(|ins| ins
                .set("group", col("source.group"))
                .set("region", col("source.region"))
                .set("val", col("source.val"))).unwrap()
            .await?;
        table = new_table;
        let active_files = table.snapshot()?.log_data().num_files();
        println!("{group:?} merge {i}: files_removed={}, active_files={active_files}", metrics.num_target_files_removed);
    }
    Ok(())
}

#[tokio::main]
async fn main() -> DeltaResult<()> {
    run("foo bar").await?;
    run("foo_bar").await?;
    Ok(())
}
RS

cat > /testbed/crates/core/examples/repro_merge_space.rs <<'RS'
use std::sync::Arc;
use arrow_array::{Int32Array, RecordBatch, StringArray};
use arrow_schema::{DataType, Field, Schema};
use datafusion::prelude::*;
use deltalake_core::kernel::{DataType as DeltaDataType, PrimitiveType, StructField, StructType};
use deltalake_core::{DeltaResult, DeltaTable};

fn delta_schema() -> StructType {
    StructType::try_new(vec![
        StructField::new("group".into(), DeltaDataType::Primitive(PrimitiveType::String), true),
        StructField::new("region".into(), DeltaDataType::Primitive(PrimitiveType::String), true),
        StructField::new("val".into(), DeltaDataType::Primitive(PrimitiveType::Integer), true),
    ]).unwrap()
}

fn source(ctx: &SessionContext, group: &str) -> datafusion::error::Result<DataFrame> {
    let schema = Arc::new(Schema::new(vec![
        Field::new("group", DataType::Utf8, true),
        Field::new("region", DataType::Utf8, true),
        Field::new("val", DataType::Int32, true),
    ]));
    let batch = RecordBatch::try_new(schema, vec![
        Arc::new(StringArray::from(vec![group, group, group])),
        Arc::new(StringArray::from(vec!["A", "B", "C"])),
        Arc::new(Int32Array::from(vec![1, 2, 3])),
    ])?;
    ctx.read_batch(batch)
}

async fn run(group: &str) -> DeltaResult<()> {
    let dir = tempfile::tempdir().unwrap();
    let table_url = url::Url::from_directory_path(dir.path()).unwrap();
    let ops = DeltaTable::try_from_url(table_url).await.unwrap();
    let mut table = ops.create()
        .with_columns(delta_schema().fields().cloned())
        .with_partition_columns(vec!["group"])
        .await?;

    for i in 1..=2 {
        let ctx = SessionContext::new();
        let source = source(&ctx, group).unwrap();
        let predicate = col("target.group").eq(lit(group))
            .and(col("target.region").eq(col("source.region")));
        let (new_table, metrics) = table.merge(source, predicate)
            .with_source_alias("source")
            .with_target_alias("target")
            .when_matched_update(|u| u.update("val", col("source.val"))).unwrap()
            .when_not_matched_insert(|ins| ins
                .set("group", col("source.group"))
                .set("region", col("source.region"))
                .set("val", col("source.val"))).unwrap()
            .await?;
        table = new_table;
        println!("{group:?} merge {i}: files_removed={}, active_files={}", metrics.num_target_files_removed, table.snapshot()?.log_data().num_files());
    }
    Ok(())
}

#[tokio::main]
async fn main() -> DeltaResult<()> {
    run("foo bar").await?;
    run("foo_bar").await?;
    Ok(())
}

cat > /testbed/crates/core/examples/repro_merge_space.rs <<'RS'
use std::sync::Arc;
use arrow_array::{Int32Array, RecordBatch, StringArray};
use arrow_schema::{DataType, Field, Schema};
use datafusion::prelude::*;
use deltalake_core::kernel::{DataType as DeltaDataType, PrimitiveType, StructField, StructType};
use deltalake_core::{DeltaResult, DeltaTable};

fn delta_schema() -> StructType {
    StructType::try_new(vec![
        StructField::new("group", DeltaDataType::Primitive(PrimitiveType::String), true),
        StructField::new("region", DeltaDataType::Primitive(PrimitiveType::String), true),
        StructField::new("val", DeltaDataType::Primitive(PrimitiveType::Integer), true),
    ]).unwrap()
}

fn source(ctx: &SessionContext, group: &str) -> datafusion::error::Result<DataFrame> {
    let schema = Arc::new(Schema::new(vec![
        Field::new("group", DataType::Utf8, true),
        Field::new("region", DataType::Utf8, true),
        Field::new("val", DataType::Int32, true),
    ]));
    let batch = RecordBatch::try_new(schema, vec![
        Arc::new(StringArray::from(vec![group, group, group])),
        Arc::new(StringArray::from(vec!["A", "B", "C"])),
        Arc::new(Int32Array::from(vec![1, 2, 3])),
    ])?;
    ctx.read_batch(batch)
}

async fn run(group: &str) -> DeltaResult<()> {
    let dir = tempfile::tempdir().unwrap();
    let table_url = url::Url::from_directory_path(dir.path()).unwrap();
    let ops = DeltaTable::try_from_url(table_url).await.unwrap();
    let mut table = ops.create().with_columns(delta_schema().fields().cloned()).with_partition_columns(vec!["group"]).await?;
    for i in 1..=2 {
        let ctx = SessionContext::new();
        let predicate = col("target.group").eq(lit(group)).and(col("target.region").eq(col("source.region")));
        let (new_table, metrics) = table.merge(source(&ctx, group).unwrap(), predicate)
            .with_source_alias("source").with_target_alias("target")
            .when_matched_update(|u| u.update("val", col("source.val"))).unwrap()
            .when_not_matched_insert(|ins| ins.set("group", col("source.group")).set("region", col("source.region")).set("val", col("source.val"))).unwrap()
            .await?;
        table = new_table;
        println!("{group:?} merge {i}: files_removed={}, active_files={}", metrics.num_target_files_removed, table.snapshot()?.log_data().num_files());
    }
    Ok(())
}

#[tokio::main]
async fn main() -> DeltaResult<()> { run("foo bar").await?; run("foo_bar").await?; Ok(()) }
RS

use std::sync::Arc;
use arrow_array::{Int32Array, RecordBatch, StringArray};
use arrow_schema::{DataType, Field, Schema};
use datafusion::prelude::*;
use deltalake_core::kernel::{DataType as DeltaDataType, PrimitiveType, StructField, StructType};
use deltalake_core::{DeltaResult, DeltaTable};
fn delta_schema() -> StructType { StructType::try_new(vec![StructField::new("group", DeltaDataType::Primitive(PrimitiveType::String), true),StructField::new("region", DeltaDataType::Primitive(PrimitiveType::String), true),StructField::new("val", DeltaDataType::Primitive(PrimitiveType::Integer), true)]).unwrap() }
fn source(ctx: &SessionContext, group: &str) -> datafusion::error::Result<DataFrame> { let schema=Arc::new(Schema::new(vec![Field::new("group", DataType::Utf8, true),Field::new("region", DataType::Utf8, true),Field::new("val", DataType::Int32, true)])); let batch=RecordBatch::try_new(schema, vec![Arc::new(StringArray::from(vec![group, group, group])),Arc::new(StringArray::from(vec!["A", "B", "C"])),Arc::new(Int32Array::from(vec![1, 2, 3]))])?; ctx.read_batch(batch) }
#[tokio::main]
async fn main() -> DeltaResult<()> { let group="foo bar"; let dir=tempfile::tempdir().unwrap(); let table_url=url::Url::from_directory_path(dir.path()).unwrap(); let ops=DeltaTable::try_from_url(table_url).await.unwrap(); let mut table=ops.create().with_columns(delta_schema().fields().cloned()).with_partition_columns(vec!["group"]).await?; for i in 1..=2 { let ctx=SessionContext::new(); let predicate=col("target.group").eq(lit(group)).and(col("target.region").eq(col("source.region"))); let (new_table, metrics)=table.merge(source(&ctx, group).unwrap(), predicate).with_source_alias("source").with_target_alias("target").when_matched_update(|u| u.update("val", col("source.val"))).unwrap().when_not_matched_insert(|ins| ins.set("group", col("source.group")).set("region", col("source.region")).set("val", col("source.val"))).unwrap().await?; table=new_table; println!("merge {i}: files_removed={}, active_files={}", metrics.num_target_files_removed, table.snapshot()?.log_data().num_files()); } Ok(()) }

    // applied more than once (for example, a partition directory
    // `group=foo%20bar` can appear in the file-id column as
    // `group=foo%2520bar`). Normalize both the raw survivor id and a
    // once-decoded form so rewritten files are removed regardless of whether

use std::sync::Arc;
use arrow_array::{Int32Array, RecordBatch, StringArray};
use arrow_schema::{DataType, Field, Schema};
use datafusion::prelude::*;
use deltalake_core::kernel::{DataType as DeltaDataType, PrimitiveType, StructField, StructType};
use deltalake_core::{DeltaResult, DeltaTable};
fn delta_schema() -> StructType { StructType::try_new(vec![StructField::new("group", DeltaDataType::Primitive(PrimitiveType::String), true),StructField::new("region", DeltaDataType::Primitive(PrimitiveType::String), true),StructField::new("val", DeltaDataType::Primitive(PrimitiveType::Integer), true)]).unwrap() }
fn source(ctx: &SessionContext, group: &str) -> datafusion::error::Result<DataFrame> { let schema=Arc::new(Schema::new(vec![Field::new("group", DataType::Utf8, true),Field::new("region", DataType::Utf8, true),Field::new("val", DataType::Int32, true)])); let batch=RecordBatch::try_new(schema, vec![Arc::new(StringArray::from(vec![group, group, group])),Arc::new(StringArray::from(vec!["A", "B", "C"])),Arc::new(Int32Array::from(vec![1, 2, 3]))])?; ctx.read_batch(batch) }
async fn run(group:&str)->DeltaResult<()> { let dir=tempfile::tempdir().unwrap(); let table_url=url::Url::from_directory_path(dir.path()).unwrap(); let ops=DeltaTable::try_from_url(table_url).await.unwrap(); let mut table=ops.create().with_columns(delta_schema().fields().cloned()).with_partition_columns(vec!["group"]).await?; for i in 1..=2 { let ctx=SessionContext::new(); let predicate=col("target.group").eq(lit(group)).and(col("target.region").eq(col("source.region"))); let (new_table, metrics)=table.merge(source(&ctx, group).unwrap(), predicate).with_source_alias("source").with_target_alias("target").when_matched_update(|u| u.update("val", col("source.val"))).unwrap().when_not_matched_insert(|ins| ins.set("group", col("source.group")).set("region", col("source.region")).set("val", col("source.val"))).unwrap().await?; table=new_table; println!("{group:?} merge {i}: files_removed={}, active_files={}", metrics.num_target_files_removed, table.snapshot()?.log_data().num_files()); } Ok(()) }
#[tokio::main]
async fn main() -> DeltaResult<()> { run("foo bar").await?; run("foo_bar").await?; Ok(()) }

use std::sync::Arc;
use arrow_array::{Int32Array, RecordBatch, StringArray};
use arrow_schema::{DataType, Field, Schema};
use datafusion::prelude::*;
use deltalake_core::kernel::{DataType as DeltaDataType, PrimitiveType, StructField, StructType};
use deltalake_core::{DeltaResult, DeltaTable};
fn delta_schema() -> StructType { StructType::try_new(vec![StructField::new("group", DeltaDataType::Primitive(PrimitiveType::String), true),StructField::new("region", DeltaDataType::Primitive(PrimitiveType::String), true),StructField::new("val", DeltaDataType::Primitive(PrimitiveType::Integer), true)]).unwrap() }
fn source(ctx: &SessionContext, group: &str) -> datafusion::error::Result<DataFrame> { let schema=Arc::new(Schema::new(vec![Field::new("group", DataType::Utf8, true),Field::new("region", DataType::Utf8, true),Field::new("val", DataType::Int32, true)])); let batch=RecordBatch::try_new(schema, vec![Arc::new(StringArray::from(vec![group, group, group])),Arc::new(StringArray::from(vec!["A", "B", "C"])),Arc::new(Int32Array::from(vec![1, 2, 3]))])?; ctx.read_batch(batch) }
async fn run(group:&str)->DeltaResult<()> { let dir=tempfile::tempdir().unwrap(); let table_url=url::Url::from_directory_path(dir.path()).unwrap(); let ops=DeltaTable::try_from_url(table_url).await.unwrap(); let mut table=ops.create().with_columns(delta_schema().fields().cloned()).with_partition_columns(vec!["group"]).await?; for i in 1..=2 { let ctx=SessionContext::new(); let predicate=col("target.group").eq(lit(group)).and(col("target.region").eq(col("source.region"))); let (new_table, metrics)=table.merge(source(&ctx, group).unwrap(), predicate).with_source_alias("source").with_target_alias("target").when_matched_update(|u| u.update("val", col("source.val"))).unwrap().when_not_matched_insert(|ins| ins.set("group", col("source.group")).set("region", col("source.region")).set("val", col("source.val"))).unwrap().await?; table=new_table; println!("{group:?} merge {i}: files_removed={}, active_files={}", metrics.num_target_files_removed, table.snapshot()?.log_data().num_files()); } Ok(()) }
#[tokio::main]
async fn main() -> DeltaResult<()> { run("foo bar").await?; run("foo_bar").await?; Ok(()) }

+    // `group=foo%20bar` can appear in the file-id column as

+    if survivors.contains(full_id.as_str()) {
+        return Ok(true);
+    }
+
+    // DataFusion/object-store paths may be materialized with URL escapes
+    // applied more than once (for example, a partition directory
+    // `group=foo%20bar` can appear in the file-id column as
+    // `group=foo%2520bar`). Compare a normalized form with double-escaped
+    // percent signs restored. Decode only `%25` -> `%`, not all percent
+    // escapes, so encoded path separators such as `%2F` remain path data.
+    Ok(survivors.iter().any(|survivor| {
+        normalize_path_as_file_id(survivor.as_str(), table_root, "merge survivor")
+            .is_ok_and(|survivor_id| survivor_id == full_id)
+            || normalize_path_as_file_id(
+                &survivor.replace("%25", "%"),
+                table_root,
+                "merge survivor",
+            )
+            .is_ok_and(|survivor_id| survivor_id == full_id)
+    }))
 }
